<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="with-overlay" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#with-overlay"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>With Overlay</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can also add a logo or overlay to the QR code. This is useful when you want to brand the QR code.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="error-correction" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#error-correction"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Error Correction</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In cases where the link is too long or the logo overlay covers a significant area, the error correction level can be
increased.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">encoding.ecc</code> or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">encoding.boostEcc</code> property to set the error correction level:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">L</code>: Allows recovery of up to 7% data loss (default)</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">M</code>: Allows recovery of up to 15% data loss</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Q</code>: Allows recovery of up to 25% data loss</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">H</code>: Allows recovery of up to 30% data loss</li>
</ul>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the QR code is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useQrCode</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_51hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_51hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_51hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="download" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#download"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Download</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">QrCode.DownloadTrigger</code> component to allow users to download the QR code as an image. Specify the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">fileName</code>
and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">mimeType</code> props for the downloaded file.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_57hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_57hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_57hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"qr-code\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cQrCode.Root\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Frame\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Pattern /\u003e\n  \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Overlay /\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.DownloadTrigger /\u003e\n\u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/react/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cQrCode.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame className={styles.Frame}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern className={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/vue/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Frame Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/svelte/qr-code'\n  import styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cQrCode.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n  \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n\u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### With Overlay\n\nYou can also add a logo or overlay to the QR code. This is useful when you want to brand the QR code.\n\n**Example: overlay**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/react/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nexport const Overlay = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cQrCode.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" encoding={{ ecc: 'H' }}\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame className={styles.Frame}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern className={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Overlay className={styles.Overlay}\u003e\n        \u003cimg src=\"https://ark-ui.com/icon-192.png\" alt=\"Ark UI Logo\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Overlay\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/solid/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nexport const Overlay = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cQrCode.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" encoding={{ ecc: 'H' }}\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Overlay class={styles.Overlay}\u003e\n        \u003cimg src=\"https://ark-ui.com/icon-192.png\" alt=\"Ark UI Logo\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Overlay\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/vue/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" :encoding=\"{ ecc: 'H' }\"\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Frame :class=\"styles.Frame\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Pattern :class=\"styles.Pattern\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Overlay :class=\"styles.Overlay\"\u003e\n      \u003cimg src=\"https://ark-ui.com/icon-192.png\" alt=\"Ark UI Logo\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Overlay\u003e\n  \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/svelte/qr-code'\n  import styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cQrCode.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" encoding={{ ecc: 'H' }}\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n  \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Overlay class={styles.Overlay}\u003e\n    \u003cimg src=\"https://ark-ui.com/icon-192.png\" alt=\"Ark UI Logo\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/QrCode.Overlay\u003e\n\u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Error Correction\n\nIn cases where the link is too long or the logo overlay covers a significant area, the error correction level can be\nincreased.\n\nUse the `encoding.ecc` or `encoding.boostEcc` property to set the error correction level:\n\n- `L`: Allows recovery of up to 7% data loss (default)\n- `M`: Allows recovery of up to 15% data loss\n- `Q`: Allows recovery of up to 25% data loss\n- `H`: Allows recovery of up to 30% data loss\n\n**Example: error-correction**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/react/qr-code'\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/radio-group'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\nimport radio from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\ntype ErrorLevel = 'L' | 'M' | 'Q' | 'H'\n\nexport const ErrorCorrection = () =\u003e {\n  const [errorLevel, setErrorLevel] = useState\u003cErrorLevel\u003e('L')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" encoding={{ ecc: errorLevel }}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Frame className={styles.Frame}\u003e\n          \u003cQrCode.Pattern className={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n        \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.Root\n        className={radio.Root}\n        defaultValue=\"L\"\n        orientation=\"horizontal\"\n        onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setErrorLevel(e.value as ErrorLevel)}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cdiv className=\"hstack\"\u003e\n          {['L', 'M', 'Q', 'H'].map((level) =\u003e (\n            \u003cRadioGroup.Item className={radio.Item} key={level} value={level}\u003e\n              \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl className={radio.ItemControl} /\u003e\n              \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText className={radio.ItemText}\u003e{level}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n              \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n            \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/solid/qr-code'\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/radio-group'\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\nimport radio from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\ntype ErrorLevel = 'L' | 'M' | 'Q' | 'H'\n\nexport const ErrorCorrection = () =\u003e {\n  const [errorLevel, setErrorLevel] = createSignal\u003cErrorLevel\u003e('L')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" encoding={{ ecc: errorLevel() }}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n          \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n        \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.Root\n        class={radio.Root}\n        defaultValue=\"L\"\n        orientation=\"horizontal\"\n        onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setErrorLevel(e.value as ErrorLevel)}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cdiv class=\"hstack\"\u003e\n          \u003cFor each={['L', 'M', 'Q', 'H']}\u003e\n            {(level) =\u003e (\n              \u003cRadioGroup.Item class={radio.Item} value={level}\u003e\n                \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl class={radio.ItemControl} /\u003e\n                \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText class={radio.ItemText}\u003e{level}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n                \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n              \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/vue/qr-code'\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/radio-group'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\nimport radio from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\ntype ErrorLevel = 'L' | 'M' | 'Q' | 'H'\nconst errorLevel = ref\u003cErrorLevel\u003e('L')\nconst levels: ErrorLevel[] = ['L', 'M', 'Q', 'H']\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" :encoding=\"{ ecc: errorLevel }\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame :class=\"styles.Frame\"\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern :class=\"styles.Pattern\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Root\n      :class=\"radio.Root\"\n      defaultValue=\"L\"\n      orientation=\"horizontal\"\n      @value-change=\"(e) =\u003e (errorLevel = e.value as ErrorLevel)\"\n    \u003e\n      \u003cdiv class=\"hstack\"\u003e\n        \u003cRadioGroup.Item v-for=\"level in levels\" :key=\"level\" :class=\"radio.Item\" :value=\"level\"\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl :class=\"radio.ItemControl\" /\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText :class=\"radio.ItemText\"\u003e{{ level }}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/svelte/qr-code'\n  import { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/radio-group'\n  import styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n  import radio from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\n  type ErrorLevel = 'L' | 'M' | 'Q' | 'H'\n  let errorLevel = $state\u003cErrorLevel\u003e('L')\n  const levels: ErrorLevel[] = ['L', 'M', 'Q', 'H']\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\" encoding={{ ecc: errorLevel }}\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n  \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n  \u003cRadioGroup.Root\n    class={radio.Root}\n    defaultValue=\"L\"\n    orientation=\"horizontal\"\n    onValueChange={(e) =\u003e (errorLevel = e.value as ErrorLevel)}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cdiv class=\"hstack\"\u003e\n      {#each levels as level}\n        \u003cRadioGroup.Item class={radio.Item} value={level}\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl class={radio.ItemControl} /\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText class={radio.ItemText}\u003e{level}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the QR code is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useQrCode` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode, useQrCode } from '@ark-ui/react/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const qrCode = useQrCode({ value: 'http://ark-ui.com' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={qrCode}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Frame className={styles.Frame}\u003e\n          \u003cQrCode.Pattern className={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n        \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.RootProvider\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003e{qrCode.value}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode, useQrCode } from '@ark-ui/solid/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const qrCode = useQrCode({ value: 'http://ark-ui.com' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={qrCode}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n          \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n        \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.RootProvider\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003e{qrCode().value}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { QrCode, useQrCode } from '@ark-ui/vue/qr-code'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nconst qrCode = useQrCode({ value: 'http://ark-ui.com' })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"qrCode\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame :class=\"styles.Frame\"\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern :class=\"styles.Pattern\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003e{{ qrCode.value }}\u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { QrCode, useQrCode } from '@ark-ui/svelte/qr-code'\n  import styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const qrCode = useQrCode({ id, value: 'http://ark-ui.com' })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={qrCode}\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n  \u003c/QrCode.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003e{qrCode().value}\u003c/output\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Download\n\nUse the `QrCode.DownloadTrigger` component to allow users to download the QR code as an image. Specify the `fileName`\nand `mimeType` props for the downloaded file.\n\n**Example: download**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/react/qr-code'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nexport const Download = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cQrCode.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame className={styles.Frame}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern className={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.DownloadTrigger className={button.Root} fileName=\"qr-code.png\" mimeType=\"image/png\"\u003e\n        Download\n      \u003c/QrCode.DownloadTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/solid/qr-code'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\nexport const Download = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cQrCode.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Frame class={styles.Frame}\u003e\n        \u003cQrCode.Pattern class={styles.Pattern} /\u003e\n      \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.DownloadTrigger class={button.Root} fileName=\"qr-code.png\" mimeType=\"image/png\"\u003e\n        Download\n      \u003c/QrCode.DownloadTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { QrCode } from '@ark-ui/vue/qr-code'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/qr-code.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cQrCode.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" defaultValue=\"http://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.Frame :class=\"styles.Frame\"\u003e\n      \u003cQrCode.Pattern :class=\"styles.Pattern\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/QrCode.Frame\u003e\n    \u003cQrCode.DownloadTrigger :class=\"button.Root\"
